< Review>
I have been getting haircuts from Eddie since 2012. He really cares about his clients. His skills on the scissors are a 10/10. He will give you recommendations based on your face structure and personality. It is super easy to make an appointment. The best part is that I always get compliments from people on the street, coworkers, ext. The place looks really nice, it has a Rock-ability theme, and it is not as intimidating like barbershops where clients are staring at each other to see which barber messes up their line-ups. I have gone to the best barber shops in Los Angeles for example Jonathan Deluxe and the quality is not the same.<//Review>

<text>My Barber's name is David. He goes by "Thy Art" for some reason; I'm guessing his Sensei gave him that name when he was just a young lad in training--or not.

<Review>You know, the first time I went to this place, I had just moved in across the street and I was trying everyone out. My girlfriend ordered the Pork Belly sandwich because she's Asian and "Hella Basic" (Her words). I don't remember what I ordered but, I think it was called the, "I'm not paying attention and this is the wrong sandwich". I wasn't impressed. It was a fine sandwich but not enough to get me back there until today, 9 months later. My girlfriend psychotically loved her sandwich because, as I mentioned earlier, SHE BASIC.

Any who, I walked in today starving, as I had skipped lunch, and I really wanted a sandwich. I carefully skimmed the menu and landed on the Amarillo by Morning. To say that this sandwich was amazing is like saying, "Nukes are a bad idea." It's just a disastrous understatement. This sandwich is the reason I will get out of bed tomorrow. It's the sandwich all other sandwiches should be measured against. The combination of flavors present reminds me of the legendary music from "Wild Stallions". Music that aligned the stars and brought about world peace. It's what we need in this world.

To summarize, when patronizing this lovely local sandwich venue, just order the AMARILLO BY MORNING! Don't hesitate. Don't deliberate. Just do it. Your perception will be forever changed. Also, this place has a great happy hour with a lovingly curated Beer list, wine list and even a cider list. All those things together make for a stop worth your while.

Tl;DR - If you don't like awesome, good things, go somewhere else.</Review><rating>5< /rating>< pictures>
None</pictures>

We have been here for about 2 months and leasing for 1yr. We (husband + baby+ cat+me) moved out (3 bdr+ 2 br) due to our other fellow sub tenants (for 5 yrs+) were leaving out of state. Where we used to live there was never really any upkeep and though the house was pretty nice we would no longer put up with quanity over quality. Back to River oaks, Clare got us thru the application process, she was friendly and professional. Alyssa and Shantel later helped answer any questions i had in office or by phone call, they are friendly, professional, and funny as well. We closed the deal in just 2 weeks after having started the process. Kat was the one who we finished signing paperwork with and she was helpful, professional and funny. We are still ecstatic about being here, this is our first apartment the only noise we hear are the typical things that people shouldn't really mind; neighbors above us, cars (we are next to freeway and you never truly hear them from inside), surprisingly light amount of barking around my unit. I'm surprised that the walls aren't "thin", i only hear footsteps and assuming cabinets/doors closing or stuff falling from my neighbors. The rent is pretty "up there" but this is the most affordable apartment on the street especially for all they offer, during late August. I've seen minimal amount of bugs in unit which is great because this season is usually teeming with bugs. I haven't seen anyone raid the dumpster in my area. Our assigned parking spot always is available to us. Outside is full of life with so many plants/trees in sync with season, birds and bugs that follow. Everyone I've encountered here is nice and keeps to themselves really which is nice too haha. So far no problems with; electricity , water, appliances (which included in unit). The upgrades (upgraded unit)and all the amenities in the complex are honestly really well done. It's a wonderful place to call home.
